#<Bayonets On Slot 2>

#<Description>

Changes accessories so bayonets never spawn on slot 1, only on slot 2, freeing up your weapon to have another accessory in addition to a bayonet. Does not despawn existing bayonets on slot 1.

Does not affect certain weapons. Certain guns – mostly uniques – now have a guaranteed accessory.

Example Guns:
Law (Now can have any accessory)
Rubi and Grog Nozzle (Your choice of always has a blade or sometimes has a blade)
Tattler (Now can have any accessory)
Cobra (Always has an accessory)
Pimpernel (Always has an accessory)

Coded by: Orudeon
With assistance from: the_Nocturni, LightChaosman

WARNING: This mod alters the fundamental spawning rules of the game. Guns that spawn with a bayonet while this mod is active violate the sanity check. Do not deactivate this mod after using it. Please run this mod as early in your load order as possible.

Please keep in mind that any mod that alters WeaponPartListCollectionDefinitions may be incompatible with this.

It is highly recommended this mod be used in conjunction with AngrierPat's Prefix Rework mod.

#</Description>

#<Pistol Bayonets>

#<Accessories>

#<Law>

#<Description>

Changes the Law's blade to be fixed to slot 2 and unlocks accessories so any non-blade accessory can spawn on slot 1.

#<Prefixes>

#<Description>

Sets all pistol bayonet titles to minimal priority. If a pistol has two accessories, the title should not display the bayonet. This code is a workaround for bayonet titles taking priority over the primary accessory.

#</Description>

#<Code>

set GD_Weap_Pistol.Name.Prefix_Torgue.Prefix_Bayonet_2 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Pistol.Name.Prefix_Hyperion.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Pistol.Name.Prefix_Dahl.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Pistol.Name.Prefix_Bandit.Prefix_Bayonet_2 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Pistol.Name.Prefix_Tediore.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Pistol.Name.Prefix_Jakobs.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Pistol.Name.Prefix_Maliwan.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Pistol.Name.Prefix_Vladof.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.4

#</Code>

#</Prefixes>

#<Prefixes>

#<Description>

Sets all assault rifle bayonet titles to minimal priority. If an assault rifle has two accessories, the title should not display the bayonet. This code is a workaround for bayonet titles taking priority over the primary accessory.

#</Description>

#<Code>

set GD_Weap_AssaultRifle.Name.Prefix_Dahl.Prefix_Bayonet_2 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_AssaultRifle.Name.Prefix_Bandit.Prefix_Bayonet_2 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_AssaultRifle.Name.Prefix_Vladof.Prefix_Bayonet_2 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_AssaultRifle.Name.Prefix_Torgue.Prefix_Bayonet_2 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_AssaultRifle.Name.Prefix_Jakobs.Prefix_Bayonet_2 Priority 0.4

#</Code>

#</Prefixes>

#</Assault Rifle Bayonets>

#</Accessories>

#<Prefixes>

#<Description>

Sets all SMG bayonet titles to minimal priority. If an SMG has two accessories, the title should not display the bayonet. This code is a workaround for bayonet titles taking priority over the primary accessory.

#</Description>

#<Code>

set GD_Weap_SMG.Name.Prefix_Hyperion.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.40000
set GD_Weap_SMG.Name.Prefix_Dahl.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.40000
set GD_Weap_SMG.Name.Prefix_Tediore.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.40000
set GD_Weap_SMG.Name.Prefix_Maliwan.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.40000
set GD_Weap_SMG.Name.Prefix_Bandit.Prefix_Bayonet_2 Priority 0.40000

#</Code>

#</Prefixes>

#</SMG Bayonets>

#<Prefixes>

#<Description>

Sets all shotgun bayonet titles to minimal priority. If a shotgun has two accessories, the title should not display the bayonet. This code is a workaround for bayonet titles taking priority over the primary accessory.

#</Description>

#<Code>

set GD_Weap_Shotgun.Name.Prefix_Jakobs.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Shotgun.Name.Prefix_Torgue.Prefix_Bayonet_2 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Shotgun.Name.Prefix_Bandit.Prefix_Bayonet_2 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Shotgun.Name.Prefix_Hyperion.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_Shotgun.Name.Prefix_Tediore.Prefix_Bayonet_1 Priority 0.4

#</Code>

#</Prefixes>

#</Shotgun Bayonets>

#<Prefixes>

#<Description>

Sets all sniper rifle bayonet titles to minimal priority. If a sniper rifle has two accessories, the title should not display the bayonet. This code is a workaround for bayonet titles taking priority over the primary accessory.

#</Description>

#<Code>

set GD_Weap_SniperRifles.Name.Prefix_Dahl.Prefix_Bayonet1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_SniperRifles.Name.Prefix_Maliwan.Prefix_Bayonet1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_SniperRifles.Name.Prefix_Hyperion.Prefix_Bayonet1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_SniperRifles.Name.Prefix_Jakobs.Prefix_Bayonet1 Priority 0.4
set GD_Weap_SniperRifles.Name.Prefix_Vladof.Prefix_Bayonet1 Priority 0.4

#</Code>

#</Prefixes>

#</Sniper Rifle Bayonets>

#</Bayonets On Slot 2>
